  <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
   var msisdn="";
		var whois="";
		if(msisdn != ""){
		   $.ajax({
			   type: "POST",
			   url: "http://www.vodafone.com.tr/CVMWhoisService.php",
			   async: false,
			   data : { msisdn: msisdn },
			   success:function(data) {
							   whois = data;
			   }
		   });
		}
		var clusterText="";
		var marketingId="";
	if(msisdn != ""){
		$.ajax({
			 type: "POST",
			 url: "http://www.vodafone.com.tr/CVMResponseService.php",
			 async: false,
			 data : { msisdn: msisdn },
			 success:function(data) {
				var cvmClusterVal = data;
				cvmClusterArr = cvmClusterVal.split("-");						
				marketing_id  = cvmClusterArr[1];
				clusterText = cvmClusterArr[0];
				marketingId = marketing_id;
			 }
		});
	}
		var headerEnch = "non-HE";
		if(msisdn != "")
			headerEnch = "HE";
		if(msisdn != "" && clusterText != "")
			headerEnch = clusterText;
		createCookie("cvm_cluster_true", headerEnch);
		createCookie("marketing_id", marketingId);
		
		function createCookie(cookieName, cookieVal){
			var now = new Date();
			var yearVal = now.getFullYear();
			yearVal = yearVal + 1;
			var cookieExpDate = new Date(now.setFullYear(yearVal));
			document.cookie = cookieName + "= " + cookieVal + ";expires= " + cookieExpDate +";path=/" + ";domain=.vodafone.com.tr";
		}

        <script type="text/javascript">
         $('#lili .login-a').on('click', function(e){
                        e.preventDefault();
                        
                            $('.login-nudge__prompt').toggle();

                            var state = $('.login-nudge__prompt').css('display');

                            if(state == 'block'){
                                $('.login-nudge__link').css('background', '#fff');
                                $('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#333');
                            } else {
                                if($( window ).width() < 768){
                                    $('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
                                    $('.login-nudge__link').css('background', '#414141');
                                }else{
                                   $('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
                                $('.login-nudge__link').css('background', 'transparent');
                                }
                                
                            }
                            $( window ).scroll(function() {
                                if($( window ).width() < 768){
                                    $('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
                                    $('.login-nudge__link').css('background', '#414141');
                                }else{
                                   $('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
                                $('.login-nudge__link').css('background', 'transparent');
                                }
                                //$('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
                                //$('.login-nudge__link').css('background', '#414141');
                            });
                            
                        });
        </script>

         $(document).ready(function(){

                    $("#tlyukle-a").mouseenter(function(){
                        $("#tlyukle-black").css("display", "none");
                        $("#tlyukle-white").css("display", "block");
                    });
                    $("#tlyukle-a").mouseleave(function(){
                        $("#tlyukle-black").css("display", "block");
                        $("#tlyukle-white").css("display", "none");
                    });

                    $("#faturaode-a").mouseenter(function(){
                        $("#faturaode-black").css("display", "none");
                        $("#faturaode-white").css("display", "block");
                    });
                    $("#faturaode-a").mouseleave(function(){
                        $("#faturaode-black").css("display", "block");
                        $("#faturaode-white").css("display", "none");

                    });
                });


                $(window).scroll(function() {

                        if ($(this).scrollTop()>30)
                         {
                            $('.fatura-ode').removeClass("hide--lg");
                         }
                        else
                         {
                          $('.fatura-ode').addClass("hide--lg");
                         }
                });

        <script>
         function openNav() {
						document.getElementById("aramaOverlay").style.height = "100%";
						$(".overlay-content").css('display', 'block');
						$(".c-overlay > .closebtn").css('display', 'block');
						$(".c-overlay").css('display', 'block');
						$('html, body').css({
						overflow: 'hidden',
						height: '100%'
						});
					}

					function closeNav() {
						document.getElementById("aramaOverlay").style.height = "0%";
						$(".overlay-content").css('display', 'none');
						$(".c-overlay > .closebtn").css('display', 'none');
						$(".c-overlay").css('display', 'none');
						$('html, body').css({
						overflow: 'auto',
						height: 'auto'
					});
					}

					$('.login-nudge-close').on('click', function(e){
					e.preventDefault();
					$('.login-nudge__prompt').hide();
					if($( window ).width() < 768){
					$('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
					$('.login-nudge__link').css('background', '#414141');
					}else{
					$('.login-nudge__link').css('color', '#fff');
					$('.login-nudge__link').css('background', 'transparent');
					}
					});
        </script>
       </ul>
      </div>

    $(document).ready(function(){
$('.tabs__tab').on('click', function(){
            var target = $(this);
            $('html, body').animate({
              scrollTop: target.offset().top - 75
            }, 1000, function() {
              // Callback after animation
              // Must change focus!
              var $target = $(target);
              $target.focus();
              if ($target.is(":focus")) { // Checking if the target was focused
                return false;
              } else {
                $target.attr('tabindex','-1'); // Adding tabindex for elements not focusable
                $target.focus(); // Set focus again
              };
            });
        });
